U.S. General MacArthur Appointed Military Advisor to the Philippines, MacArthur, a Proponent of War Against Japan, Determined to Train Philippine Army for Ten Years 58

(Tokyo) Former U.S. Army Chief of Staff General MacArthur, a known proponent of war against Japan in the United States, has been hired by the new government of the Philippines to serve as military advisor to the Philippine Army. When passing through Japan and Hong Kong, he avoided meeting with reporters. Even when meeting with those who welcomed him, he remained silent and refused to speak. MacArthur's purpose in this trip is to implement a ten-year plan to train the Philippine Army so that it will become a powerful force capable of resisting the enemy. (19th Hualian Telegram)

Bloodless Sanctions Against a Militarist Country: An Innovation in League of Nations History 59

Fifty-Two Countries Sever Economic Relations with Italy, Rome Remains Calm, No Xenophobic Disturbances

(Geneva) The first day of the League of Nations' sanctions against Italy began at midnight today. In world history, this is an innovation in using bloodless methods to punish a militaristic country. A total of fifty-two countries are participating in the sanctions. The four other members of the League of Nations whose economic positions are not very important – Austria, Albania, and Paraguay – have refused to participate. France has stopped importing Italian silk, and Cuba has refused to import Italian fruits and olive oil. British Malaya and the Dutch East Indies have boycotted Italian rubber. Yugoslavia, Iran, and Egypt have refused to supply Italy with mules, camels, and food. Sweden and Russia have stopped selling raw materials such as nickel and magnesium to Italy. Banks around the world have also stopped lending to Italy. (18th National Telegram)

(London) Except for some student demonstrations in Burma against sanctioning countries which resulted in minor conflict, in the major cities of Italy, no foreign hatred happened today when the League of Nations members began implementing economic sanctions. The British Embassy and others in Rome were all protected by military forces, preventing incidents. There are now over 50 nations who are fulfilling their obligations in accordance with Article 16 of the League of Nations treaty, forbidding the shipping of goods to and from Italy. Although Egypt is not a member, they have notified the League of Nations that they are prepared to act in the same way. At the same time, the governments of Germany and the United States, who are not affiliated with the League of Nations, have also adopted measures to facilitate the actions of the member nations. According to dispatches from Geneva, Argentina has notified the League of Nations Secretariat that they are currently forbidding exports of major commodities such as petroleum and steel. Geneva insiders deem Argentina's decision as extremely important as this act will lead to member nations limiting exports to Italy, especially oil products, through concerted action. The British Treasury has issued orders pertaining to economic sanctions in the past few days, stipulating that debts owed to Italian exporters should be delivered to the newly appointed British-Italian debt administrator, and stipulating that any goods imported into the UK must be accompanied by a certificate of origin to prevent Italian goods from being mixed in. France has implemented sanctions against Italy through government orders, forbidding Italian goods from being imported into French territory, and banning the transportation of raw materials listed by the League of Nations Commission to Italy. French veterans have nominated representatives to visit Prime Minister Laval at the end of the week to protest against the implementation of sanctions. Laval replied that on the one hand, he advocates that France fulfills its obligations under the alliance agreement, and on the other hand, will continue to strive to promote a peaceful resolution as soon as possible. In addition, there has been no formal statement from France. The transportation of goods on Italian railways is currently very scarce. Many trains have now been suspended in order to save coal. Trading on the Rome Stock Exchange is also limited due to the uncertain situation. An Italian government spokesperson today asked journalists to publish in newspapers the situation of the Italian people remaining calm even in times of provocation. (18th Reuters Telegram)

Supreme Council of the Fascist Party Adjourns 60

Awaiting Military Progress in East Africa, Reconvening on the 18th of Next Month

(Rome) The Supreme Council of the Fascist Party continued its meeting yesterday evening at 10:00, ending only at 1:00 this morning. According to the communique, "Prime Minister Mussolini presented a report on military and political affairs, lasting for more than two hours." Following the Prime Minister, the speakers were: Grandi, the Ambassador to the UK, reporting on the public opinion situation after the completion of the UK House of Commons elections; Air Force General Balbo, the Governor of Libya in Africa (Britain has requested the Italian government to recall him to his home country); Thaon di Revel, the Minister of Finance; Marconi, the Senator and radio inventor (who recently made an invention said to be astonishing regarding motorized warfare); Volpi, the President of the Senate; and Farinacci, the former Secretary of the Fascist Party. The current session of the Supreme Council of the Fascist Party has ended and is scheduled to reconvene on the 18th of next month. It is said that the next month will be a period of "waiting." Regarding military affairs in Africa, the detachments commanded by Generals Maravigna and Pirzio Biroli are currently engaged in mopping-up operations in the Danakil Alps area and have not yet concluded the affair. The Italian army may not immediately engage in large-scale operations. Regarding diplomacy, there is currently no progress. Prime Minister Mussolini's recent discussions with British Ambassador Drummond concerned the Mediterranean issue and were unrelated to the Abyssinian incident. This conversation only achieved psychological progress. Italian sources believe that if a major military victory is achieved, a new environment will be created, and diplomatic work will naturally become more convenient. (19th Havas Telegram)

Italian Government Resists Sanctions, Promulgates New Import and Export Regulations 61

(Rome) The government has recently promulgated new import and export regulations in order to resist sanctions. The main points are as follows:

(1) Regarding exports: (A) The export of all Italian necessities is prohibited, except for those specially permitted by the Ministry of Finance. (B) The export of non-necessities that are not being shipped to countries implementing sanctions is still permitted as usual, but must be presented with a bank endorsement. (C) Goods being shipped to countries implementing sanctions must also be presented with a bank endorsement. This endorsement should be issued in accordance with the following conditions: (1) The exporter has obtained a loan from an Italian bank. (2) The payment for the goods has been paid in advance and has been remitted to an Italian bank. (3) Those who wish to export wool, cotton, silk, or other goods have obtained permission from the relevant specialized bureau for those goods. (2) Regarding imports: (A) A special permit must be obtained to import necessities. (B) Luxury goods imported from countries not implementing sanctions should be allowed to be imported in accordance with the quantity imported at this time last year, with a prescribed percentage rate. (C) Any goods from countries implementing sanctions are not permitted to be imported. (18th Havas Telegram)

US Strictly Adheres To Neutrality Law, Maritime Shipping Is Not Protected, Maritime Union Resolves Not To Take Risks 62

The United States St. Peter's, Pacific Maritime Union announced today that the union's seafarers will not agree to work on American ships loaded with military supplies bound for the Italian-Ethiopian war zone. This move has created a new development in the US attitude toward the Italian-Ethiopian conflict and the European crisis. The Department of Commerce had previously announced that trade with belligerent countries is against American policy and stated that American diplomacy does not protect maritime shipping in wartime. Now the union's spokesman then stated that after the ship sets sail, Britain and France may have already started war with Italy, so the union has made this resolution. As for the dockworkers along the Pacific coast, they do not intend to interfere with loading cargo onto foreign ships bound for the war zone. However, since the government does not protect American ships, why order American seafarers to take this risk? At the same time, the cargo ship Oregon, fully loaded with gasoline bound for Manila, Shanghai, and Singapore, has not yet set sail because the seafarers are unwilling to work on the ship before obtaining an affirmative reply from Secretary of State Hull that protection will be provided. (18th National Telegram)

Goodstein, The American International Trade Association convened a meeting today. Simpson announced the thesis of retired Rear Admiral Phelps, saying that if the US embargo on Italian goods were expanded to include raw materials, it would be an unfriendly gesture towards Italy. If Britain uses the name of sanctions to illegally blockade Italy, resulting in the interception of American goods at sea, then the American people will not submit. The chairman of the meeting was Frankel, the former chairman of US Steel. During today's meeting, those present had quite divergent opinions on the issue of trade with Italy and sanctions. Mr. Fei's thesis advocating the continued protection of transport by the United States, received unanimous approval in the meeting. Furthermore, Fei's discussion on the Far East issue, saying that the independence of the Philippines has caused complex situations on both sides of the Pacific and the Mediterranean, also received great attention from the audience. Fei said, "The United States is digging its own grave, and has allowed Britain's old friend, Japan, to confine the US Navy to one corner of the Pacific, weakening its national defense in the Atlantic direction, and leaving the gateway to the commercial routes of the Atlantic wide open. In fact, these commercial routes are more important to the American people's livelihood than Manchuria. If the League of Nations were to announce a blockade of Italy, then America's Atlantic commerce would be completely at the mercy of others." Former US Ambassador to Chile, Culbertson, opposed Mr. Fei's views, saying that the US should support the League of Nations' sanctions against aggressor nations. (18th National Telegram)

Italy Protests Sanctions, England and France Discuss Replies 63

New Italian Commander Goes to East Africa, Hoping to Conquer Abyssinia Quickly 65

Abyssinian King Departs to Lead Troops in Person, Soldiers Anxious to Serve, Preparing to Resist the Enemy

(Rome) The newly appointed High Commissioner to East Africa and Commander-in-Chief of the Italian forces, General Badoglio, together with his two sons (one an air force officer, one an artillery officer) and Deputy Governor of Eritrea, General Gusani, and others, recently arrived at the Port of Naples. They will board the "Sunnia" steamship tonight to take up their new posts in East Africa. (18th Havas Telegram)

Abyssinian Capital: The appointment of General Badoglio as Commander-in-Chief is seen as a sign that the Italian army will engage in offensive operations with a large-scale plan. Until now, the Italian army has been operating cautiously, so progress has been slow, and no major battles have been seen. Italy is clearly changing its strategy because various countries are now implementing sanctions against Italy. Its military leaders may have received instructions to conquer Abyssinia as quickly as possible in order to avoid prolonging the war, which would cause Italy to feel the impact of economic sanctions and be detrimental to the war effort. (18th Reuters Telegram)

Abyssinian Capital: The Abyssinian Emperor departed by plane today to lead the troops in person, and will go to Taishi or Harar to command the army. (19th National Telegram)

Asmara: It was learned today that a large Abyssinian army has departed for Selihodylik, 10 miles from Magal, preparing for formal resistance. It is expected that the Italians and Abyssinians will engage in a fierce battle near Magal. (19th National Telegram)

Abyssinian Capital: The Italian forces in East Africa are temporarily suspending their offensive until their new Commander-in-Chief General Badoglio arrives, while the Abyssinian army is actively preparing for its first real resistance. It is rumored in the Abyssinian capital that the Abyssinian King will soon personally go to the northern front to encourage the soldiers. Today, sixteen trucks left for the Taishi Abyssinian army base, twelve of which were fully loaded with the Abyssinian King's personal items. The remaining trucks were equipped as Red Cross ambulances and managed by an Austrian doctor. It is believed that the Abyssinian army is still holding the strongholds of Dagabu and Sasabani on the Worgaden Line. Reports regarding these two places are often conflicting. However, the fall of Gola Hai has been admitted by non-official sources. It is said that the Abyssinian army abandoned the town as a tactical maneuver to free up troops to defend against the Italian army advancing along the Tafan River. It is also heard that the Abyssinian army is preparing to fiercely defend against the Italian army attempting to occupy some freshwater wells southeast of Sasabani. (18th Reuters Telegram)

Italian Army Exterminates Humanity, Engages in Extensive Aerial Bombing 66

Bombs Fall Like Rain, Abyssinian Army Suffers Over a Thousand Casualties, Italian Prime Minister's Son-in-Law Directs Massacre

Asmara: Italian aircraft carried out the largest attack since the start of the war yesterday, fiercely attacking the Abyssinian army's defenses built in the Mewehafe and Memsestik valleys south of Magal, destroying many military supplies. Twenty heavy bombers participated in the operation, including Mussolini's son-in-law Count Ciano and Mussolini's two sons. The planes left Asmara early yesterday morning. Several hours later, they spotted the enemy, numbering about 15,000. At the signal, the planes descended to less than a hundred feet from the ground, dropping two-pound bombs and strafing with machine guns. The Abyssinian army immediately scattered, but at least hundreds were hit before they could run to shelter. The attack lasted for two hours. The Abyssinian army responded with anti-aircraft guns and machine guns. Ciano, after returning from battle, reportedly told a Reuters reporter that his plane had been hit by anti-aircraft shells three times and by rifle and machine gun bullets thirty-six times. Other planes were hit an average of ten times. The fuel tank of his plane had been pierced by a bullet and he was forced to land in Magal. One of the pilots in his plane had his leg bone shattered by a bullet, but he still used his thumb to plug the bullet hole in the fuel tank, allowing the plane to continue flying. (19th Reuters Telegram)

(Rome) Officials here announced today that in yesterday's large-scale Italian air attack on the Abyssinian army's defenses in the Mewehafe and Memsestik valleys south of Magal, only two Italians were injured. The planes dropped a total of six tons of bombs. According to unofficial estimates, no fewer than a thousand Abyssinian soldiers were killed. (19th Reuters Telegram)

Tigre Province Front: The correspondent of this newspaper traveling with the army, Bal News, reported that between the Anami-Xiaer City and the city east of Magal, and the Meiweixi River and Meiweili River, there were two thousand Abyssinian army troops. Italian air force units launched an unexpected attack, launching no less than six thousand kilograms of bombs. The Abyssinian army death and injury count is around six thousand. It was the most fierce aerial attack since the beginning of the war. The Abyssinian army defended themselves using rifles and machine guns, but did not shoot down a plane. Prime Minister Mussolini’s son-in-law also participated in the war personally. Midway through the flight, the engine of his plane started leaking oil. He was forced to land in Magal. The only one injured was a pilot named Billago. Mussolini’s two sons also engaged in the war by flying a plane. The machine guns they carried ran out of ammunition, therefore they shot at the Abyssinian forces using their rifles. (19th Havas Telegram)

Two Italian Columns Advance Eastward in Northern Route 67

Tigray Front: Bal, a reporter of this newspaper traveling with the army, reports that the Italian army is now advancing eastward in two columns towards Danbian City. It is likely that the Abyssinian General Sai Xiong's heavy forces stationed there will resist the Italian army. The first column started from Magal City, and the second column started from Gangdi Mountain and has occupied the Akello Pass. It is reported that the Italian army previously sent outposts to reconnoiter in front of Danbian, but they encountered a large Abyssinian army, so they retreated immediately. In addition, a portion of the Second Army Group is searching for enemy troops in the Natir area. Another Blackshirt regiment is camped near Abakahan. According to air reconnaissance, there are large Abyssinian forces in the Meweharu and Attala areas, and an Abyssinian column is advancing north between Andami Xiaan and Buga City. It is also heard that the Italian authorities in Aduwa City have established a committee to adjudicate cases for the native people of Abyssinia. The committee is composed of local gentry and nobles. (18th Havas News Agency Telegram)

De Bono Bids Farewell to His Troops 68

Abyssinian Capital: The outgoing Italian Army Commander-in-Chief De Bono bid farewell to his subordinates today. His staff gathered outside the general's tent. The general shook hands with each of them and gave a short speech, thanking them for their loyal assistance and encouraging them to treat his successor with the same attitude. Then, escorted by a cavalry detachment, he traveled by car to Asmara. (18th Reuters Telegram)

Large Abyssinian Army Cuts Off Enemy's Rear 69

Magal: Three battalions of Italian indigenous troops rushed to the eastern part of the Danping area today to defend against the Abyssinian army. It is because Sai Xiong, the commander of the Abyssinian Northern Route, leading 30,000 troops, after being in hiding for several weeks, suddenly appeared in the Danping area. According to today's news, the Abyssinian army has built high walls and deep trenches in the mountains between Magal and Aduwa, and has the latest weapons. However, military experts are baffled as to how General Sai Xiong was able to move a large army behind the advance troops of the Italian army. (19th National Telegram)

Egyptian Nationalist Party Appeals to League of Nations, Accusing Britain of Obstructing Independence and Showing Aggression 70

Cairo: Nahas, the leader of the Egyptian Nationalist Party, sent a telegram to the League of Nations Secretariat today, strongly opposing British actions in Egypt and requesting the League of Nations to act as a referee between independent countries and aggressor nations. The telegram stated that the Egyptian government had recently proposed concluding a mutual agreement with Britain to guarantee each other's interests, with Egypt joining the League of Nations as one of the conditions of the agreement. However, this proposal was rejected by Britain, which proves that Britain does not want Egypt to implement the 1923 constitution and benefit from it, or that it certainly does not want Egypt to enjoy real independence. (19th Reuters Telegram)

(Geneva) The League of Nations Secretariat received telegrams today from the Egyptian Nationalist Party and the Cairo Student Union, opposing the British government's attitude towards the Egyptian constitution. Both telegrams were informal in nature and were not published. However, it is heard that the telegrams also complained about the Egyptian government's heavy-handed treatment of student demonstrations and supported Egypt's application to become a member of the League of Nations. At the same time, the turbulent situation in Egypt seems to have hindered the negotiations between Britain and Italy regarding the Mediterranean. Although sanctions against Italy have been implemented, it is widely believed that both Britain and Italy feel that the Mediterranean issue should be resolved as soon as possible. Therefore, observers believe that Britain and Italy will make new efforts to reach an agreement in the near future. (18th Reuters Telegram)

French Radical Party Submits New National Defense Budget, Totaling 69 Billion Francs 71

(Paris) The new national defense budget proposed today by Mr. An Bao, the leader of the Radical Socialist Party in the Chamber of Deputies, stated that Germany currently has 800,000 soldiers in service, including 530,000 regular soldiers, 30,000 armed police, 40,000 auxiliary troops, and 200,000 labor troops. Mr. An also predicted that this army would reach one million within a few months. The new French national defense budget allocates a total of 6,953,674,380 francs for military expenditures. (18th National Telegram)

England and Soviet Russia Negotiate Commercial Loans: Russia Borrows from England to Buy English Goods 72

(London) According to financial circles, the British and Soviet governments began negotiations today to have Britain grant commercial loans to the Soviet Union, so that trade relations between the two countries could be established on a solid foundation. Considering the general economic situation of the Soviet Union, there is a desire to see improvement, and the recent Soviet government order to stabilize the ruble price, stipulating that each ruble is equivalent to three French francs, further proves the success of the Soviet government's currency system reform. Therefore, trade relations between Britain and the Soviet Union will inevitably be smoother from now on. For several years, the British government has repeatedly taken various measures to promote British-Russian trade. This time, the two countries have begun negotiations again, hoping to borrow from Britain to purchase British goods for the Soviet Union. It is expected that the negotiations will have successful results. As for officials, they are unwilling to release detailed information, only saying that the purpose of today's negotiations is to extend loans to the Soviet government for the purpose of purchasing railway materials from Britain. This type of commercial loan has recently also been granted to the Soviet Union by Germany. In this negotiation, the government will inevitably take into account the interests of British bondholders of bonds issued during the Tsarist era. (Havas dispatch on the 18th)

Head of the US Study Mission Advocates Investing in China, Saying Strict Conditions Caused Missed Opportunities 73

Huston, Forbes, the head of the American Far East Economic Study Mission, said today in a speech to the China-America group of the American National Foreign Trade Council that the United States has lost a good opportunity to invest in China due to strict lending conditions. We really need to quickly establish credit bureaus in China and give American businessmen good opportunities in China. The US Treasury's silver purchase policy has greatly tightened China's currency, but the Chinese people still very much welcome the United States to participate in their business. The council also sent a telegram to Shanghai to congratulate the Sino-American Commerce 150th Anniversary Conference. (National Telegram on the 18th)

German Novelist Arrested in England on Suspicion of Espionage 74

(London) It was learned today that the German novelist Goetz recently arrived in Harwich, England, from Europe, and was found to be hiding documents that violated the Official Secrets Act. He was arrested by the British secret intelligence team and charged with espionage. He is now imprisoned in London and will be tried in a few days. According to reports, Goetz previously studied medicine in Edinburgh and served in the German Air Force during the European War. (Reuters dispatch on the 19th)

Japanese Consulate in Hankou Holds Meeting on the Upper Yangtze 77

The meeting lasts for two days, presided over by Japanese Consul General Miura. The Japanese side claims it is to improve relations between the two countries.

Hankou Correspondence: Japanese Ambassador Arita, considering that the upper reaches of the Yangtze River are in a crucial location, has ordered all consuls stationed in Sichuan, Hunan, Henan, and Jiangxi to gather in Hankou to hold a joint meeting on the 18th and 19th to discuss everything in detail, and has appointed Miura, the Japanese Consul General in Hankou, to be responsible for convening the meeting. On the 17th, Tanaka, the Consul General in Jiujiang, Takai, the Consul General in Changsha, Sonobe, the Consul in Shashi, Kasuya, the Consul General in Chongqing, Shibasaki, the Consul in Yichang, and Sakusui, the Consul General in Zhengzhou, all arrived in Hankou. At 10:00 AM on the 18th, the meeting was held at the Japanese Consulate General. Military attachés and secretaries of the Japanese Navy and Army stationed in Hankou attended the meeting, totaling more than 20 people. Chairman Miura reported on the situation of the previous consular meeting in Shanghai, and the gist of the Japanese Foreign Ministry's intention to improve Sino-Japanese relations as stated by the head of the Ministry's Guarding Islands Section. Then, consuls from various places reported on the situation of overseas Chinese merchants in their respective areas. The meeting adjourned around 12:00 noon. In the afternoon, they attended a grand banquet held by the Japanese community. It was decided to continue the meeting on the 19th to discuss all important cases. It was adjourned on that evening. After the meeting, the discussion will be telegraphed to Japanese Ambassador Arita. It is said that according to the Japanese side, the purpose of this meeting is to listen to reports from various places and seek friendship between the two countries, and nothing else. (18th)

Shen Baixian Reports on Flood Prevention Efforts in Northern Jiangsu 78

More than one million laborers mobilized in each county, Disaster area losses exceed 10 million yuan.

Zhenjiang News: Shen Baixian, Director of the Department of Construction, reported on the flood prevention efforts in Northern Jiangsu at the Joint Party-Government Memorial Week on the 18th, saying: "Since the Yellow River breached its banks on July 10th until now, it has been more than four months. According to statistics, in these four months, the number of people and civil servants in various counties who participated in flood prevention work has exceeded one million. The district-by-district report numbers are as follows: (1) Tongshan District (Tongshan, Peixian, Pizhou, Fengxian): A total of 390 kilometers of embankments were built, with 4,560,000 cubic meters of earthwork, mobilizing 480,000 laborers. (2) Counties along the Central Canal (Suqian, Siyang, Lianshui, Huaiyin): 300 kilometers of embankments were built, with 2,100,000 cubic meters of earthwork, mobilizing 300,000 laborers. (3) Counties along the Liutang River (Shuyang, Donghai, Guanyun): 250 kilometers of embankments were built, with 4,180,000 cubic meters of earthwork, mobilizing 280,000 laborers. A total of 940 kilometers of embankments were built in eleven counties, with 8,950,000 cubic meters of earthwork, and 1,060,000 people were mobilized. As for its effectiveness, the west embankment of Weishan Lake is 120 kilometers long, which is enough to prevent water from invading the west. The Henaan embankment is 100 kilometers long, which was built from the Huaiyin District, and is enough to prevent water from invading the south. The Liuyang-Donghai Dike is 100 kilometers long and is built along the highway, serving as a barrier to protect Donghai and Shuyang counties. This embankment project was extremely fast, taking no more than 15 days at most, and some were completed in just 10 days. Although the flood has subsided somewhat now, according to the past water levels at Hanzhuang, the highest was only 36.5 meters, but this year the highest reached 37.00 meters, and it is currently still between 36.4 and 36.5 meters. The breach has not been plugged, and the flow rate is still more than 2,000 cubic meters per second. Considering the evaporation in the middle and the capacity of Weishan Lake, at 1,000 cubic meters per second, the downstream flow exceeds the standards set by the Economic Commission by a large margin. If the breach plugging problem is solved, it can be completely retreated within two months. The counties affected by this disaster include Tongshan, Peixian, Pizhou, Fengxian, Suqian, Siyang, Lianshui, Shuyang, Guanyun, Donghai, etc., with a disaster area of ​​approximately more than 8 million mu. Comparing it with the situation in the 10th, 15th, and 20th years of the Republic of China, the period is longer and the disaster is more severe, but due to effective protection, the disaster area only accounts for one-fifth. Although autumn crops have been harvested, winter crops cannot be planted. 8 million mu of farmland have been flooded, and at 10 yuan per mu, the loss is 80 million yuan. Adding the loss of houses, etc., it should be more than 100 million yuan. Now, in addition to hoping to plug the breach as soon as possible, the post-disaster engineering and relief work are particularly urgent. Because the Huai River has little water this year and the Bengbu water level is only 15 meters, if the Huai River and Yellow River floods occur together next year, the situation in Northern Jiangsu may be more serious than it is today."

Economic Commission Handles Agricultural Projects in Jiangxi Province 79

Appropriates 500,000 Yuan

Jingde Correspondence: The rural areas of this province have been devastated by bandits for a long time, and most are dilapidated. The National Economic Commission considers that with the banditry pacified in various counties, the revitalization of the rural areas of this province is an urgent task. A special fund of 500,000 yuan has been approved to handle rural cooperative undertakings, and the Jiangxi Cooperative Fund Management Committee has been organized to take charge. Regarding the loan areas for this year, in addition to the original 25 counties, JInxi, Yujiang, Lianhua, Yongfeng Suichuan, Leping, Qianshan, Guixi, Shanggao, Wanzai, Yichun, Nanfeng, Xiushui, Nancheng, Lichuan, and other 15 counties have been added. The loan policy includes credit, utilization, supply, transportation, and warehousing. Credit loans are mainly based on agricultural loans, and the loan amount is set at 300,000 yuan. Regarding utilization loans, 100,000 yuan has been set aside, limited to small-scale utilization businesses, mainly agricultural production, agricultural manufacturing, and farmer sideline businesses. Regarding supply and marketing loans, 100,000 yuan has also been set aside, mainly to supply members with production supplies and quickly sell specialties. (November 14th)

Zhangzhou-Sui Command Consultant Wu Zhi's Family Member Also Killed 80

Xiamen Correspondence: Wu Ci, the famous leader of the Tenth Army in Zhangzhou, was appointed as a consultant to the Sui Command after surrendering last year. On the afternoon of the 15th of this month, Wu took a rickshaw from his private residence to visit friends on Dongmen Street. He suddenly realized that there were people following him in front and behind. Realizing that something was wrong, he hurriedly got out of the car and was about to rush into the Hongji Rice Shop, but four thugs had already approached and fired four shots with Mauser pistols. Wu was hit by one bullet and was about to draw his gun to fight back when he was shot several more times and collapsed on the steps, dying instantly. Seeing that Wu was dead, the four thugs and other thugs stopped a car, got in, and urged the driver to drive away quickly. The police on duty heard the sound and rushed to the scene, but it was too late. They immediately reported to the Third Resident Office by telephone and rushed to the scene of the murder to investigate. They saw that Wu had been shot five times and died, lying in a pool of blood. The Sui Command is strictly investigating the case, and the City Defense Department has ordered the Debt Collection Office and the 478th Regiment to strictly arrest the murderers. The 478th Regiment dispatched dozens of soldiers by car to Guokeng to investigate. Wu is survived by a wife, four concubines, and five sons, and was 41 years old. Three hours after the Wu case occurred, a passenger car No. 136 from Zhangnan drove from Punan to Zhangzhou. When the car arrived at Nankeng Shekou, three people shouted to stop the car, twisted two passengers off the car, and opened fire, shooting randomly until the two passengers fell to the ground, and the three thugs fled. After the thugs left, other passengers got off the car to check and saw that one person was dead and the other was seriously injured. They sent the injured person to a local hospital for treatment. According to the injured person, his name is Yu Shu. He received a telegram from the family of Wu (Ci), the consultant, saying that Wu had been assassinated and asked him to bring money to Zhangzhou. So he and Liu Shenyuan brought more than 800 yuan and came by car. Unexpectedly, they were attacked by a gun. Liu had been killed, and the money had been taken. In the evening, Yu also died of his injuries. The 478th Regiment also dispatched troops to Punan to investigate and arrest the murderers. (November 16th)

Bandit Den Cracked Down in Qingdao 81

Two bandits killed and five captured on the spot; patrol officer and three policemen also injured

Qingdao Correspondence: Because of the strict military and police defense in Qingdao and effective household registration inspections, the local area has always been peaceful. However, due to the recent economic panic and rural bankruptcy, villagers have no way to make a living and have resorted to desperate measures, resulting in frequent kidnapping cases in various places. Qingdao has also been affected. On the 31st of last month, two robbery cases occurred in Dongtaiping Village. Wang Shize, Director of the Public Security Bureau, believing that robberies had occurred during the winter defense period, issued a general order to all district teams to investigate. At about 5:00 PM on the 14th of this month, two bandits, Liu Shouwen and Wang Zongwen, were wandering back and forth on the road near the Dazhanshan Temple, intending to rob. It happened that two forest policemen from the Agricultural and Forestry Office were passing by and saw that the two bandits were acting suspiciously, so they stepped forward to question them. The bandit Wang Zongwen, seeing that the situation was not good, fired a shot at the forest policeman and fled in a hurry. Another bandit, Liu Shouwen, was unarmed and was arrested on the spot. After a brief interrogation by the Agricultural and Forestry Office, he was sent to the Fourth Branch of the Public Security Bureau for interrogation. However, the bandit Liu was extremely cunning and refused to tell the truth. Later, the Fourth Branch escorted him to Dongtaiping Village to be identified by the robbery victims. It turned out that he was the bandit who committed the robbery with a gun. The bandit, seeing that there were witnesses, had no way to deny it and confessed that he had an accomplice named Liu Yuegong, who currently lives at No. 18 Caoxian Road. So they went to the address to arrest him. The bandit Liu jumped out of the back window to escape but was also captured. According to Liu, he is from Shanxian County, 25 years old. Because the situation in his hometown was not good, he came to Qingdao to find work. On the evening of the 31st of last month, Wang Zongwen and others invited him to commit a crime, so he went to Dongtaiping Village. After the incident, he only received one yuan. Now, Wang Zongwen, Zhang Zigang, and five others are hiding at No. 27 Zhongjiawa, with three pistols, etc. After taking the confession, Ling Han, Director of the Fifth Branch, led patrol officer Meng Dexuan and chief police officer Hao Huajun, etc., to arrest them by police car at 11:00 PM on the 14th. It was late at night and the sky was dark. Patrol officer Meng Dexuan and police chief Dai Shouheng and others bravely climbed over the wall. At this time, the bandits in the house were already awake and opened fire from inside the house. At the same time, the police officers also returned fire. After a long battle, patrol officer Meng and policemen Zhang Dazhu and Pei Dengshan were all injured and fell to the ground. Director Ling still supervised the police to move forward bravely. Then, police officer Zhou Jijin risked breaking into the house and hugged the bandit Wang Zongwen, who was carrying a gun. At the same time, Director Ling also led the police to break in. The bandits were all captured, and the bandits Li Zikui and Liu Shenwu were killed on the spot (both of the above bandits were injured by gunfire). Zhou Zhenqing was also captured. The injured patrol officer Meng Dexuan was hit by three bullets, one bullet passed through his right arm, one bullet grazed his right breast, and one bullet passed through his left shoulder. Policemen Pei Dengshan's left wrist was pierced by one bullet, and Zhang Dazhu's right shoulder was pierced by one bullet. All were sent to Zhongwen Hospital for treatment. The robbery case in Dongtaiping Village was thus solved. (16th)

Songjiang 82

Another Suspect Apprehended in Car Robbery Case

In the case of the bandit robbery on the Shanghai-Hangzhou Highway near Yanggong Temple, the Water Patrol Team and the Security Team have jointly arrested and interrogated the principal offenders, Zhang Xiaobaogen and He Xiaoshang. The remaining bandits are still being hunted. Patrol officer Sun Zuoqing of the Caoging Ninth Resident Office learned that Lu Bojun, a resident of No. 11, Sixth Jia, Fourth Bao, Huqiao Township, was suspected of colluding with the car robbers. He led the police to arrest him for interrogation at the county bureau. According to the confession, he is 88 years old, from Shaba Tu, and has an elderly mother at home. He usually only gambles with He Xiaoshang and others at home. I did not participate in the car robbery. It was indeed done by someone and his apprentices Zhang Xiaobaogen and others. I did not get any of the stolen money. However, on the fourth day of the tenth lunar month this year, I took six or seven long and short guns with someone to rob the homes of Mei Daohang, Mei Xingting, and Gu Jisheng in Sunjiaqiao, Fengxian County, and divided three yuan, etc. The bureau feared that the suspect would evade the car robbery and downplay the seriousness of the crime, so it decided to detain him for further investigation.

Suzhou 83

College Student Arrested for Trafficking in Opium

Tao Zhaorong, a student from a university in Shanghai, from Jiangxi, 25 years old, came to Suzhou from Shanghai on the 18th, carrying a large amount of opium. He stayed at No. 58, Dongwu Hotel, Dama Road outside the Lvmen Gate. The matter was discovered by the police district in charge. At about 8:00 PM, inspector Cui led a team of police officers to arrest Tao Zhaorong. More than 100 taels of opium were found in his luggage and he was taken to the district and transferred to the general bureau. Later, on the 19th, he was sent to the County Anti-Smoking Association for further investigation. Zhao Ming, who was in contact to purchase the opium, escaped during the chaos and is now being hunted.

County Government Forms Field Rent Public Judgment Office

The landlords in Suzhou have successively opened warehouses to collect rent. However, it has been five days since the warehouses opened, and the harvest has not improved, and the total amount is less than 20%. The landlords, in order to show consideration for the tenants, extended the first payment deadline by ten days. In order to handle the disputes between landlords and tenants, the county government specially organized the Field Rent Public Judgment Office and hired local impartial people to serve as committee members. It will be established within a few days. In the future, all disputes between landlords and tenants will be handled by the office for public judgment. If there is any dissatisfaction, they can formally file a lawsuit with the court according to the law. However, matters concerning tenants' rent arrears will be decided by the county government through administrative adjudication and are not within the scope of public judgment to avoid conflicts with the law.

Changzhou 84

Resolution to the Shizhuang Case

The reconnaissance team sent by Wujin to Shizhuang (under the jurisdiction of Jiangyin County) to arrest bandits, which resulted in casualties, has been resolved. The provincial government believes that the reports from the two county governments are inconsistent. They have twice sent people to investigate and have clarified the facts of the case. It was learned yesterday that the province has decided on a resolution: (1) The arrest procedures on the Wujin side did have omissions. (2) The Chengguan County is ordered to capture the wanted bandit Peng Shengrong and bring him to justice. (3) The local township Baoczhang should be severely punished as a warning to those who harbor bandits. The above decision will be ordered to be followed by the two counties. The Shizhuang bandit arrest and injury case during the chaotic times will be concluded in this way.

Nantong 85

Township Security in Six Counties of Nantong

Banditry has been rampant in the township areas of the six counties of Nantong in recent days. Xu Zhen, the Nantong District Commissioner, believes that the crux of the banditry lies in the fact that the government has not planned for prevention, and the people lack the ability to organize self-defense, so that bandits and petty thieves take the opportunity to steal. He has formulated the Township Security Implementation Measures for each county, stipulating that household registration should be strictly enforced, the Baojia system should be used for investigation, and patrol teams should be organized with townships as units. On the one hand, the police of the Public Security Bureau and the Security Team should maintain close contact. The special commissioner will send officers to the townships of each county at any time to carry out random household registration checks and patrols.

Zhang Xiaoruo's Third Daughter Commits Suicide

Zhang Canwu, the third daughter of Zhang Xiaoruo, who was killed in Shanghai, was 16 years old and a student at Nantong Middle School. She suddenly committed suicide by poisoning on the night of the 18th. The reason is unknown. It is rumored that it was a family quarrel and she took her life out of anger. By the time it was discovered, it was too late to save her. She has been coffined and placed with her father's coffin in the Zhang family's home.

Gaoyou 86

People's Education Center Collects Winter Clothing

The Lake West Tuerji People's Education Center in this county received instructions from the Education Bureau to quickly collect winter clothing to help the disaster victims. It immediately organized a winter clothing collection team, prepared various propaganda materials and picture posters, and publicized them to the basic education area and the promotion area. They also collected donations from house to house in Taji Town, Jingu Town, and Minqiao Town. In total, they collected 504 pieces of winter clothing, 101 hats, and 160 pairs of shoes. The items were immediately packed into packages, a list was prepared, and it was submitted to the Education Bureau for transfer to the Flood Relief Sub-Committee to be sent to the disaster area for distribution.

Hangzhou 88

Construction of Jiuxi Park Begins

The Hangzhou Municipal Government, in order to enhance the scenery of the urban area and attract tourists from all over the world, is building Jiuxi Park in the Jiuxi Shiba Jian area of ​​West Lake as a place for Chinese and foreign people to relax. It has also re-divided the boundaries between Hangzhou City and County, transferring more than 30,000 mu of mountainous land from Hangzhou County to the jurisdiction of the city. The transfer procedures have been completed. Construction of Jiuxi Park has begun, including planting trees and flowers and building pavilions, etc., which can be completed within the year. Opening of the stream swimming pool and adding mountain roads will continue to begin next spring.

Filling the Hundred Lions Pool to Rebuild the Vegetable Market

The former Fan Office's Hundred Lions Pool in Hangzhou has always been inhabited by turtles. In the past, during the spring and summer seasons, they would float on the surface of the water. Foreigners would often visit the giant turtles and throw them cakes to watch them eat as a game. In recent years, the turtles have almost all died and the pond water has become dirty. The Hangzhou Municipal Government sent workers to fill the pond and rebuild the vegetable market. From now on, the story of watching turtles in the Hundred Lions Pool has become a thing of the past.

The fourth session of the Ningbo Chamber of Commerce's Member Representative Assembly commenced on the morning of the 16th. The elected Supervisory Committee members were: Mao Jiasheng, Yuan Duanfu, Hong Chensheng, and Chen Ruxin, totaling four individuals. The alternate Supervisory Committee members were: Zhang Kangchu, Zhang Zunfu, and Zhou Fuchu, totaling three individuals.

Pinghu 90

Appeal of the Jiahe Daily Libel Case

The Jiahe Daily of this city, previously reported on the discovery of a female corpse in the Pinghu city river, with rumors suggesting she was the daughter-in-law of a certain Li woman. The newspaper, along with others, adopted this piece of news. Subsequently, the daughter-in-law submitted a complaint to the county government, and the rumors subsided. The newspaper also published a clarification. However, an illiterate Li woman inexplicably filed a complaint with the county government, solely accusing the Jiahe Daily of publishing inaccurate information that damaged her reputation. The county government accepted the case, summoned both parties, and initially proposed mediation. However, with a change of county magistrate during a hasty handover, the Jiahe Daily was abruptly sentenced to a dual punishment. The newspaper company, dissatisfied with the verdict, has appealed to the Hangzhou County District Court. The court has accepted the appeal and scheduled a preliminary hearing on the 20th to thoroughly investigate the matter.

Jiaxing 91

Re-checking Household Registration to Investigate Smokers

The Jiaxing County government, in order to eradicate the harm of opium, has formulated "Implementation Measures for Opium Prohibition," assigning responsibility to Baojia chiefs to report opium users. Those who conceal or fail to report will be charged with harboring criminals. Additionally, with labor service and construction projects about to commence, the county has dispatched personnel to survey rivers, ports, streets, and other areas within each district that require dredging. Construction will begin once the survey is complete. Furthermore, the organization of strong young men into teams is a matter of urgency. Moreover, the government will be conducting personnel registration and has ordered all townships and towns to conduct a thorough re-check of household registration, while also investigating opium users to limit and force them to quit, thereby eradicating opium addiction.

Impressions of a Trip to Guangxi 92

— Qian Hua

I am recording the convenience of my previous trip with the Sixth Academic National Body conference in Nanning, Guangxi, for sightseeing in the South. On July 30th, I departed from Shanghai on the President Coolidge liner, and on August 30th, I returned to Shanghai from Hong Kong on the President Lincoln liner. The journey lasted exactly one month. The round trip passed through Hong Kong, Guangzhou, and Sanshui, but I only stayed for two or three days. Eighty percent of the trip was spent in Guangxi Province, from the commercial center of Wuzhou to the political center of Nanning, then to Longzhou to inspect the border defense facilities, and out of Zhennanguan, across the border to Lang Son in Annam, then back to Nanning, then to Liuzhou, and finally to the cultural center of Guilin. I traveled south along the Li River, passing through Yangshuo, Pingle, and Zhaoping, and then returned to Wuzhou. I traveled by boat for five days and by car along the Guangxi Provincial Highway for six days, covering more than 10,000 li in winding and rushing routes. I have been to all eight districts of Guangxi Province, except for Baise and Tianbao. People say it's a fleeting glance, but the reporter turned the fleeting glance into a racing car. The shadowy black images flew past. There's no way to talk about any impressions, but based on the oral descriptions of the local people and the general phenomena, I have taken the sightseeing and visits as a reference to synthesize my personal impressions and write them down as the conclusion of this trip to Guangxi.

First, Guangxi's clean politics starts from the highest authorities. The top leads by example and works hard. It is truly admirable. Chinese politics is very simple. As long as civil officials are not greedy for money and military officers are not afraid of death, the government will be clean and the world will be peaceful. The Guangxi authorities recognize this point and practice it themselves. On the one hand, they strive to promote thrift from the root and strictly prohibit public officials from gambling, whoring, and other bad and luxurious habits. From the commander-in-chief, deputy commander-in-chief, chairman, and department heads to the clerks, all wear the same gray homespun uniforms and hats, with no difference from ordinary people. The provincial chairman, Huang Xuchu, is often seen running on the street, and the commander-in-chief, Li Zongren, riding alone near the city is very common. This kind of gray cloth uniform costs two and a half yuan a set. An American advisor also took off his stiff, high-grade woolen suit and wore a gray cloth Western-style suit, saying to everyone that it was cheap and comfortable. This proves that customs can change psychology. Since public officials have abandoned all bad habits, their personal lives are naturally extremely simplified. A monthly salary of one or two hundred yuan is enough to cover expenses, so they will not risk their lives to engage in corruption. The so-called radical measure is that all officials in Guangxi Province dare not take a penny other than their own salaries. It is also possible to be incorruptible only after being thrifty.

Second, Guangxi's militia training starts with the lower-level farmers, doing everything practically, not seeking form, and completely eliminating the drawbacks of military-civilian alienation. The spirit of dry work is most fully manifested in the training and organization of the militia. The village militia is the foundation of the organization. The village chief serves as the captain of the militia reserve team and the principal of the national elementary school, combining military, administrative, and educational affairs. The village chiefs are graduates of middle school or above, have received rigorous training, and are all promising young people with innovative minds. There is absolutely no fact of local bullies and evil gentry taking the militia's banner to bully good people. They speak kindly and guide the villagers with sincerity, so they are all very dedicated, understand the meaning of teamwork and public interest, the lazy become diligent and thrifty, and the fierce turn into kind. From self-defense and autonomy, it is promoted to a self-sufficiency policy. The success of the Guangxi militia, in the most obvious facts, is the elimination of bandits throughout the province, the sharp reduction of beggars, and the completion of more than 30,000 li of highways. Now the self-defense power of the militia throughout the province is increasing day by day. The number of troops in Guangxi is the smallest in the country, with only five divisions, but according to military experts, the self-defense power of the province is greater than any other province, and it can resist the invasion of 500,000 of the latest type of troops. The Communist bandits who窜桂 last year were quickly wiped out, entirely by the power of the militia. Many people who went to Guangxi to visit and returned said that the Guangxi militia was indeed well organized, but most people have a kind of doubt, that is, whether the Guangxi militia training method can be extended to other provinces, especially the more affluent people in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces who are used to comfort. Because Guangxi is barren and the people are poor, the people are accustomed to hard work and are absolutely able to obey orders. As long as there are leaders, they can be tightly organized and serve the public. In Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces, the situation is exactly the opposite. If hard training is implemented, requiring farmers to run dozens of miles at dawn to gather for training, and also to take on guard duty at ordinary times, and also to take time to cultivate public fields and build roads, at the beginning of implementation, there will inevitably be complaints, and the drawbacks of substitution and exile will emerge endlessly, and local tyrants and evil gentry will emerge to obstruct it, and the difficulties will be greater than in Guangxi. But the reporter's personal opinion is that as long as the leader is determined and can lead by example everywhere, to seek factual improvement and not just seek superficiality, then there is nothing difficult in the world. It is unreasonable and impossible for the militia to be successful in Guangxi but not be able to be extended to other provinces.

Third, from the perspective of construction work, Guangxi Province now has only more than 27 million yuan in annual income, of which 60-70% still relies on special transit taxes, so the authorities act according to their income and are very cautious. Large-scale construction projects can be said to be absolutely non-existent. If you go to Guangxi with the eyes of a big city, you will be disappointed if you want to see factories and material equipment worth tens of millions. This is exactly the opposite of the situation in Guangdong. In Guangdong, there are newly established factories worth millions of yuan, and even palace-style buildings such as the Sun Yat-sen Memorial Hall and the municipal government have cost millions of yuan. But one thing is worthy of our praise. Although the amount of money Guangxi spends on construction is small, it is very economical. When one yuan is spent, the general public can enjoy the benefit of that one yuan. According to the places the reporter has visited, such as the livestock breeding institute, the agricultural experiment field, the tung oil refinery, the health experiment institute, and the public museum, they can all directly contact the public. The cost is not much, but the effect is great. It is enough to correct our country's problem of talking about construction and wasting money.

Fourth, regarding the equipment of the southwest border defense, the reporter went to Longzhou to see it once. The mountains are overlapping, and the passes are steep and dangerous. There is indeed a natural situation where one man guards the pass and ten thousand men cannot enter. At that time, Li Pinxian, the border defense superintendent, who is now the chief of staff of the Fourth Army Group, had been in office for three years and was able to revitalize border affairs and make many improvements. The training of the military militia is full of vigor. Although the defense of various important passes on the border is in the peaceful days of today, there has been no phenomenon of slackening at all. The commercial exchanges between Chinese and French merchants on the border and the joint celebrations of military and diplomatic officials from both sides can all be based on the principle of absolute equality. People who have been accustomed to being bullied go to the border and breathe the air of equality and freedom, and they really feel an unspeakable pleasure. Now Longzhou's transportation is becoming more and more convenient. There are three air flights every week, flying from Guangzhou to Wuzhou, Nanning, and Longzhou. It only takes one day to get there. There are also highways and waterways. Longzhou, which was previously regarded as a mysterious area, is now thriving in all industries, which is very different from the past. The area of the southwest border defense is full of mountains and ridges, with a sparse population. There are many miasma epidemics. Every time it is the turn of spring and summer, epidemics are prevalent, and deaths are rampant. Therefore, the number of residents is decreasing day by day, and the land is mostly barren. The reason why the border area cannot be developed is here. Currently, the Guangxi authorities are making every effort to pay attention to health administration, believing that miasma is a tropical disease and malaria, and are sending personnel to the four townships to inject prevention. There have been considerable results. In the future, we can further pay attention to the issue of immigration. The scenery of Longzhou is not inferior to Guilin. If the authorities can pay attention to cleaning it up, the future development is unlimited. Our country has always paid little attention to border defense. In 1929, the reporter went to the three northeastern provinces to inspect. The corruption of border defense in the northwest to Hailar and Manchuria was shocking. Since the September 18th Incident, it has gradually aroused the attention of the people of the country, but Ban Hong and Ban Nong are not clear, which has become a great joke. The northwest and southwest are important gateways for our country. We especially hope that the Guangxi authorities can continue to work hard and not be satisfied with the current situation, and pay as much attention as possible to the consolidation of border defense and the development of the rural economy of the border people, so that our country can resist foreign enemies and gain the first victory, and the Zhennanguan, which has unparalleled glorious value in history, will last forever with our people.

The 150th Anniversary of Sino-US Trade Was Celebrated Last Night, With 200 Chinese and American Guests Attending. Minister Kong and Others Gave Speeches 93

The celebration of the 150th anniversary of Sino-US trade was held at the American Club on Fourth Avenue at 8 PM last night. Distinguished guests from all walks of life in China and the United States, including Gu Weijun, Guo Bingwen, Chen Zhezheng, Yu Hongjun, He Bingxian, Wen Yuqing, Xu Xinliu, Chen Bingzhang, Pan Guangjiong, US Ambassador Johnson, US Commercial Counselor Arnold, US Consul General Kenningham, US Consul Davis, and others, totaling more than 200 people, attended. The event was presided over by Franklin, President of the American Chamber of Commerce, and Zhang Gongquan. The details are as follows:

Financial Minister Kong's Speech

The American Club was焕然一新 (completely renewed). The Chinese and American flags were hung in the hall. After the guests were seated, the chairman gave a speech reporting on the significance of celebrating the 150th anniversary of Sino-US trade. Then, Chen Bingzhang, Secretary of the Ministry of Finance, gave a speech on behalf of Minister Kong Yongzhi, titled "China and the United States." He elaborated on the increasingly close progress of the two countries in commerce since Sino-US trade began in 1785, with American goods accounting for the first place in China's import trade. In addition, regarding Sino-US relations, in terms of education, a large number of students go to the United States to study every year. In terms of politics, such as the Boxer Indemnity and tariff autonomy, all are sufficient to prove the intimacy of Sino-US relations. He hopes that these two peace-loving Eastern and Western countries will become more friendly in the future.

US Ambassador's Speech

Next, US Ambassador Johnson gave a speech on the early stages of Sino-US trade. Our country's Minister to France, Gu Weijun, gave a speech on various hopes for the future of Sino-US trade, with a view to developing the resources of both countries, exchanging commercial needs, and reversing the economic catastrophe. Finally, US Commercial Counselor Arnold gave a speech on various aspects of Sino-US trade. After the speech, there were various recreational activities and magic performances.

Mayor's Congratulatory Message

Mayor Wu Tiecheng, due to attending the Fifth Plenary Session, was unable to come to Shanghai to participate, so he sent a telegram to the Secretary-General of the Municipal Government, Yu Hongjun, which read: "I regret that I am unable to return to Shanghai due to official business to participate in the grand event. I sincerely wish the 150th anniversary of Sino-US trade to have a profound impact on us, proving the friendship between the peoples on both sides of the Pacific in the past, and hope that China and the United States will become more intimate and understanding in the future and strive for cooperation." Wu also sent a telegram from Beijing to Franklin, President of the American Chamber of Commerce, congratulating him (extract): "I respectfully wish this great commemoration of the 150th anniversary of Sino-US trade to deeply leave the impression of the friendship between the two countries in the hearts of the people of China and the United States, and to work more actively to increase the closeness of understanding and cooperation in the future, and congratulate the members of the American Chamber of Commerce and the Sino-US Trade Association on their health, Wu Tiecheng."

Minister Chen's Congratulatory Message

Minister of Industry Chen Gongbo also telegraphed He Bingxian, Director of the International Trade Bureau, to convey his congratulations, which read: "Since 1785, Sino-US trade has gradually increased. By 1932, it accounted for 22% of China's imports. Regarding imported goods, kerosene, steel, machinery, cotton, and wood are the main items. Exported goods include silk, preserved eggs, plants, and seeds. The import and export balance is quite uneven. In the future, I hope that the trade between the two sides will become more balanced, taking into account the mutual interests of the two countries and the changes in actual needs, so as to seek commercial interests and closely cooperate to enhance friendship." It is heard that Thomas of the American Chamber of Commerce also telegraphed from the United States to congratulate.

Roosevelt's Broadcast

At the same time, the Seattle Chamber of Commerce in the United States also held a similar banquet, and said that President Roosevelt would give a long-distance radio broadcast speech to both Shanghai and the United States at the same time (Shanghai time at 11 PM), and could be broadcast locally after receiving it by radio.

Duan Qirui's Life in Shanghai

Entertaining Himself With Buddhist Scriptures and Weiqi Every Day

According to the National News Agency, Duan Qirui, who came to Shanghai as a recluse a few years ago, has a very leisurely attitude and spends his time entertaining himself with Buddhist scriptures and Weiqi. He suffered from foot disease before, but now he has fully recovered. Yesterday, the reporter visited his residence. Duan was playing Weiqi with Weiqi masters Gu Shuiru and Wang Yunfeng. Guo You'an, a subordinate, received the reporter on his behalf and asked about Duan's life. According to him, Duan has been living in the south and does not ask about any politics. His family in Tianjin has come south since Duan was ill before. There is no real estate in Tianjin and Gu, and there is only one house in Peiping. At present, only a few gatekeepers stay there to take care of the house. Duan's daily life is to get up at 6:00 in the morning, wash, and take a walk in the garden, and then have breakfast. Because he likes Buddhism all his life, he reads Buddhist scriptures for an hour after meals, and then plays Weiqi with his close friends. After lunch, he takes a nap to rest his mind, and then meets guests if there is anything to do, and plays Weiqi if there is nothing to do, which has become a routine. Even most of the visitors are rejected and not seen. As for his foot disease, it is rheumatism accumulated in the army when he was young, and it often occurs when he gets old. If he encounters abnormal weather, he will also suffer a little pain, but it is not a big deal. Duan Zihonggang was recently sent to Anqing to invigilate the examination. Duan is 71 years old this year. Chairman Chiang Kai-shek built a house in Huangshan and invited Duan to live there. At that time, it was just to use the beautiful scenery of Huangshan as a summer resort in the hot summer. However, the weather is cold now, and the house has not been completed yet, so he will never go to Anhui to live there.

Zhejiang Construction Department Secretary Wang Yingbin Discusses the Promotion of the Cotton Industry in Zhejiang Province: This Year, Over 120,070 Mu of Cotton Fields Were Promoted, and the Results of Improved Cotton Varieties Are Significant, with Further Expansion Planned for Next Year 104

The Shen Shi News Agency reports: The Construction Department of Zhejiang Province has spared no effort in promoting various construction projects in recent years. The construction of highways and the commencement of the Qiantang River Bridge have facilitated transportation. In recent years, attention has been focused on rural construction, such as promoting cooperative farming, and improving the silk and cotton industries. The work related to cotton industry improvement is mainly handled by the Cotton Industry Management Office of the department. Its main task is to promote improved cotton varieties to meet the needs of domestic textile production. The quality of Zhejiang cotton is poor, and the fibers are too short. The annual production can only supply daily household use. Last year, the provincial government allocated a large sum to promote improved varieties. As the cotton planting and sales season comes to an end, the province's improvements have been quite effective. We met with Mr. Wang Yingbin, Secretary of the Zhejiang Construction Department and Director of the Cotton Industry Management Office, during his business trip to Shanghai. Our reporter paid a special visit to inquire about the details of the process, which are described as follows:

Many Difficulties During the Promotion Period

According to Mr. Wang, the large-scale promotion of the cotton industry in Zhejiang Province only began last year. Fortunately, this year's harvest is quite satisfactory. In total, the area of improved cotton fields reached 120,074 mu. Considering the land area of Zhejiang Province, the scope is not small. The work process was quite arduous. Cotton brokers, bound by traditional ideas, had doubts, opposition, and resistance to the improvement of the cotton industry. However, the provincial department had long-term trials of improved cotton varieties. The purpose was to seek benefits for cotton farmers and increase national production. The Management Office could only devote all its efforts to it. In addition to training and guiding more than 50 people before the event, and assigning them to various experimental areas to implement instructions and persuasion, the advantages of improved cotton and the results of historical experiments were compiled into small booklets in simple language and distributed for publicity to facilitate promotion. Although the results were good, there were also many misunderstandings. Some cotton farmers gathered crowds to destroy the offices of experimental stations, some scolded and insulted instructors, and some even resorted to violence. Some used local newspapers to attack in writing. However, the Management Office, bearing the mission of improving rural areas, had to use various methods to vigorously promote it.

Three Aspects Hindered Improvement

The reasons for the cotton farmers' obstruction were lack of common sense and greed for petty gains. In the past, the quantity of cotton harvested was arbitrarily falsely reported to reduce rental payments. Since the government was in charge, it was necessary to report truthfully, so they were unwilling to change varieties. Or they believed that although the quality of improved cotton was better, under the government's guidance, tax collection was inevitable, so they held conservative attitudes and did not seek improvement. The reasons for the obstruction by cotton brokers were that they could no longer issue high-interest loans to farmers. Generally, farmers, tempted by the availability of money to borrow and rice to buy on credit, often owed a lot to the cotton brokers. If farmers accepted improvements, the cotton brokers would inevitably force them to repay their debts. Therefore, the general farmers, under the instruction of the cotton brokers, rose up to oppose the improvements. As for the cotton field landlords, their cotton fields were usually managed by local bullies, who were often managers of cotton brokers. Thus, they spread rumors such as the government's unified collection of cotton was unfavorable to the cotton field landlords. All of these things hindered the improvement of cotton planting.

Slight Twists and Turns Were Smoothed Out by Persuasion

The reason why the office was able to solve various obstacles in the past was that it was able to obtain the cooperation of the county magistrates of various counties, who went to the countryside together for persuasive guidance. It was also fortunate to receive support from gentry and gentlemen such as Mr. Yu Qiaqing, so the cotton farmers were relieved to receive seeds and sow. However, it took a lot of effort.

Purchasing Seeds and Distributing for Planting

The office promoted improved cotton varieties. In addition to the million cotton seeds supplied by the Zhejiang Cotton Field, all the acclimatized American cotton seeds were purchased by me from Zhengzhou and other places and distributed to various planting areas. The purchase price was quite high. Although we were fortunate to have the Ministry of Railways reduce the freight charges to four yuan per dan, farmers used local cotton seeds worth one yuan to exchange for improved seeds, so the provincial government's loss on seeds was already considerable.

Number of Mu Promoted and Cotton Seed Areas

The promotion area is divided into six implementation areas and two cooperative cotton fields. The promoted area totals 120,074 mu, of which 63,181 mu are planted with million cotton, and 56,893 mu are planted with acclimatized cotton. The distribution of each area can be divided into the following table:

Area Cotton Field Area (Mu) Cotton Variety

Xiaoshan Cotton Industry Improvement Implementation Area 24,248 Million Cotton

Yuyao Cotton Industry Improvement Implementation Area 29,502 Stone Weir Million Cotton 23,672 Mu Xinpu Coast Acclimatized American Cotton 5,830 Mu

Hang County Cotton Industry Improvement Implementation Area 15,261 Million Cotton

Zhenhai Cotton Industry Improvement Implementation Area 26,524 Acclimatized American Cotton

Cixi Cotton Industry Improvement Implementation Area 19,678 Acclimatized American Cotton

Haiyan Cotton Industry Improvement Implementation Area 3,150 Acclimatized American Cotton

Yinxian Cooperative Cotton Field 1,209 Acclimatized American Cotton

Dinghai Cooperative Cotton Field 502 Acclimatized American Cotton

Improved Cotton Varieties Outperform Local Cotton

The improvement work in each area is guided by instructors appointed by the office. All planting processes must be reported in a timely manner. From the statistics, it is known that the yield of million cotton and acclimatized American cotton is generally higher than that of local cotton. The increase in yield per mu averages 70 to 80 jin, and the minimum increase is also 20 to 30 jin. The average price of million cotton and acclimatized cotton is also higher than that of local cotton. From these statistics, it can be seen that the improved seeds have achieved the desired effect. Cotton farmers should have nothing to say at this point. A comparison of the yield and price per mu of improved cotton and local cotton is detailed in the following table:

Improved Cotton Yield and Price per Mu Local Cotton Yield and Price County Highest Lowest Average Price Highest Lowest Average Price

Jin Jin Jin Jin Jin Jin

Xiaoshan 125 80 101 9.50 35 17.3 28.2 8.80

Yuyao 150 100 120 1.00 21 30 70 8.90

Hang County 80 40 60 95 80 50 10 19 9.00

Zhenhai 160 40 120 9.40 90 35 60 9.10

Haiyan 110 80 115 9.10 50 10 30 9.00

Cixi 230 70 80 9.10 90 30 60 9.30

Dinghai 160 75 210 9.60 88 40 78 8.90

Yinxian 110 110 130 9.89 42 77 9.00

Experimental Cotton Areas All Reported Bumper Harvests

When Mr. Jiang spoke to this point, the reporter asked because he had seen a report in the newspaper a few days ago about the national cotton production statistics released by the National Cotton Control Association, which said that Zhejiang Province's harvest this year was only 20%. According to Mr. Wang, the statement that Zhejiang Province's harvest this year was only 20% may be incorrect. Even in the experimental area of the improved cotton fields of the office, although it was not a bumper harvest, the gains were more than 20%. In the Hang County area, excessive fertilization led to particularly lush branches and leaves, coupled with excessive rainfall, resulting in a lower yield than in other areas. However, this is a special situation. Compared with the yield of local cotton in the same area, it is still 10 to 20 jin higher. If the entire province's production is statistically analyzed, the harvest of improved cotton is at least between 50% and 60%, and local cotton is also between 40% and 50%.

The Ministry Approves Banks and Native Banks to Receive Legal Tender, Which Will Facilitate Turnover After Implementation

The method of receiving legal tender still follows the old precedent of 60% cash and 40% bonds. The two industry associations have notified members to comply.

The Xin Sheng News Agency reports: After the Ministry of Finance ordered the silver and native banks associations to receive legal tender in accordance with the original method of receiving notes, the banks and native banks have all proceeded in accordance with the regulations. The market has become more active. The details are as follows:

Silver and Native Banks Receive Legal Tender

After the notes of the Bank of China, the Bank of Communications, and the Central Bank were designated as legal tender, the secret notes of the three banks were gradually withdrawn, which greatly affected the business of small banks and native banks that used the secret notes to conduct important business. They had to change their business policies. Now, in order to invigorate the market and facilitate the business of various banks and native banks, the Ministry of Finance has approved the receipt of legal tender in accordance with the original method of receiving notes. The silver and native banks associations have notified members to comply and have posted public notices in the market to inform the public. The various banks and native banks have all complied with the order to receive legal tender from the Bank of China, the Bank of Communications, and the Central Bank.

The Market Becomes Active After Implementation

According to a Xin Sheng News Agency reporter, for example, Article 2 of the Regulations of the Preparation Inspection Committee for the Issuance of Bank of China Notes stipulates that Bank of China exchange notes are divided into three types: issued by the bank, received by joint banks, and received by various banks and native banks. All have sufficient cash reserves of 60%, with the remaining 40% in other forms. The receipt of notes by various banks and native banks remains the same as before. Now, when banks and native banks receive legal tender from the Bank of China, the Bank of Communications, and the Central Bank, they still use 60% cash and 40% public bonds or treasury bills. The discounted price of public bonds and treasury bills is handled according to the previous regulations of the three banks. After implementation, the market has become more active.
