Little Western Heaven 201

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter 21: Tender and Gentle, She Takes Pity on His Moonlike Face; With Passionate Zeal, He Trains His Son-in-Law, Listening to the Roar from the Next Room

After listening to him, Zhiqian put his hands behind his back and kept pacing back and forth in the room. Smiling and nodding, he said, "I'm afraid you don't know the details of this matter. People will submit to anything for money. Even that guy named Jia, you see him strutting around with his nose in the air, thinking he's a big deal. But one day, for the sake of money, when someone wants to oppress him, he will have to endure it. I'll give you an example," he said, lowering his voice, "a little bureau chief has just moved into the room next door, also a compradore-type figure. He was very comfortable in Jiangnan, but for the sake of money, he went to Gansu and served as the head of the tax bureau in a very difficult place for a year. It doesn't matter that he goes to suffer. His fashionable wife in Jiangnan sent a telegram, summoning him to Xi'an to meet. The bureau chief arrived here a day earlier, and yesterday, his wife also came. In the evening, because there were no electric lights, the couple had a quarrel. The wife first said that she wanted him to send money to Xi'an. The bureau chief said that he came in a hurry and didn't have time to raise funds. If she wants money, she can go to Gansu with him. The wife anticipated the hardship and hasn't agreed yet. However, I think she will definitely go. The reason is very simple, because there is money in that place." Saying this, he smiled. At this moment, he saw a young woman in a Western suit, her high heels clicking on the ground as she passed by. Her upper garment was pink, covered with a short, thin blue woolen coat. Below was a sapphire blue skirt, swaying as she walked, with great charm. There are not many women in Xi'an who have their hair cut short, and her hair is curled in waves. Although he didn't see the woman's face, he could say with certainty that she was very beautiful. Immediately, he heard the woman speaking angrily in the next room. (364)

The Straight Crease of Western Trousers 202

— Hu Dexian

We often see people wearing Western suits, and they always like to have a very straight crease ironed on their trousers, facing the front and back. To maintain this crease for a long time, they mostly use serge or wool as the clothing material. I ask, how does this crease come about, and what is its purpose? I think everyone must want to know about this!

It is said that this was during the time when George Washington, the first elected President of the United States in the 18th century, was in office. Once, the presidential palace held a meeting, and all the congressmen arrived at the venue, but Washington had not yet arrived. After several reminders, Washington hurriedly changed into newly washed clothes and came to the venue. The crowd saw that the president's clothes had neat creases, and they all followed suit. This accidental imitation opened the way for the fashion of ironing very obvious creases on Western suits in later generations.

There are many such things. For example, recently, fashionable women in Shanghai paint their cheeks yellow, imitating a foreign movie star. From this, it can be seen how closely the actions of celebrities are related to social customs and folkways. It can also be inferred that many social phenomena are not exhaustively understood, but most are the result of this accidental imitation. Therefore, many problems that cannot be solved recently are attributed to this principle!

Places Visited

Improvised Notes on Mount Huang (Part 2) 203

— Chen Xiaodie

The beauty of Sanhua Dock must be seen from in front of the Brush Rack Peak, facing the Three Great Buddhas on the left, the Stone Bamboo Shoot Ridge on the right, and Rongcheng Peak in front. Only by sitting and admiring the blooming brush can the magical scenery be truly revealed. The wonders seen from Beginning-to-Believe Peak can all be seen from Sanhua Dock, but the wonders of Sanhua Dock cannot be seen from Beginning-to-Believe Peak. However, the mountain path has been blocked for a long time, with brambles and thorns all over the mountain, as tall as people, and the mountain mud is slippery and offers no foothold. I followed Master Weiqing in climbing up and sliding down, falling and rolling. Fortunately, we reached halfway, but we still hadn't reached the old site of Sanhua Temple. Yi Yan said that opening this road would cost no more than a hundred yuan, but I think this road should be divided into three paths: one descending from the Blooming Dream Brush to view the waterfall, one descending from the Lower Liu Pavilion to view the stone bamboo shoots, and one ascending from Songgu Temple to view the Dragon Pool. Then the hidden treasures of heaven and earth can seem to be fully revealed. I sincerely hope to work with those who have the intention to accomplish this.

The imposing scenery of the West Sea is magnificent, with towering cliffs and countless doors. In my opinion, it is the best of Mount Huang. What is particularly striking is that on the West Sea Gate, in the Pine Forest Ridge, all ten thousand pine trees grow together, with four branches connecting each other, mostly as thick as a person can embrace, completely different from the Tian Du Lotus. Azaleas and rhododendrons are especially abundant like a sea. If it were springtime, the brilliance would be indescribable. Such a magical scene is not even mentioned in the Mount Huang map. I think that if this place were developed to accommodate new village construction, so that every family could lean on the pine trees with connecting branches and sit in the sea of azalea flowers, it would add another beautiful tale beyond the Peach Blossom Spring of Wuling.

Those who carry people up Mount Huang are not well-trained, so their gait is not very neat. The construction of mountain sedan chairs is best in Mount Tai, but the porters are unrivaled in Mount Lu. Those who are considered difficult on Mount Huang, if entrusted to the porters of Mount Lu, would be as effortless as walking on flat ground. However, the sedan chairs of Mount Lu are carried by four people, so if one person falls, there are still six feet to hold on. Even if two people in the front and back fall, it is the same as the sedan chair on Mount Huang. Mount Tianmu, though easy, is also carried by four people. This is worth learning from.

Mount Huang is more than 7,000 feet high, but the sunrise can only be viewed from Bright Summit. From Wen Shu Monastery, the view is blocked by Jade Screen Peak, and from Qingliang Terrace, the view is blocked by Rongcheng Peak. Moreover, there is no shelter from a single oak tree on Bright Summit, and if one stays overnight near Lion Grove, the cold will be unbearable. I propose building a stone staircase on Jade Screen Peak to reach the top of Jade Screen, so that the sunrise will become a "Salt Pond," properly located at the "Heavenly Capital" and surely offer spectacular views. Moreover, it is close behind Wen Shu Monastery, which reduces the hardship of the journey and yields a great achievement in sightseeing. Yi Xin is convinced that its value is no more than a hundred gold.

The Mount Huang renovation has been economical and has achieved great things, but it relies on donations from mountain monks, which easily makes tourists hesitant. I think the collection books in each temple can be abolished. But in places where scenery needs to be arranged, verbal guidance should be given to allow elegant gentlemen to voluntarily donate, and the construction drawings and development locations must still be approved by the Construction Committee. Wouldn't that be good? I once calculated that building a stone staircase on Jade Screen Mountain would allow people to view the sunrise, opening a mountain path on Sanhua Dock would allow people to fully see the wonders of Stone Bamboo Shoot Ridge and Beginning-to-Believe Peak, and building five stone houses south of Qingliang Terrace would allow tourists to rest and enjoy the sea of clouds. I discussed this with Monk Xin Ding of Wen Shu Monastery and Monk Weiqing of the forest, and the total cost of this plan would be about 3,000 yuan in legal tender, which could be completed. However, in this time of economic decline, it is difficult to raise funds independently, and tens of millions of people nationwide are waiting for disaster relief, so I am unwilling to focus solely on leisurely sightseeing, which is not urgent. Therefore, I intend to spend a month creating fifty paintings, and use half of the proceeds from the sale of the paintings to fund disaster relief, and use the other half to help fund the construction of Mount Huang. I wonder if you gentlemen of great refinement can help me achieve this goal?

Records of Fragrant Mists of the Imperial Court 204

— Originally written by Princess Der Ling of the Qing Dynasty, translated by Qin Shouou

Reader's Note

— Qin Shouou

"Records of Fragrant Mists of the Imperial Court," a novelistic account of the private life of Empress Dowager Cixi of the late Qing Dynasty, finally finished its serialization yesterday. It was serialized for a total of 459 days, because not much could be published each day, which dragged it out for so long.

From the perspective of those of us who study novels, this book is indeed quite valuable. At the very least, it is very interesting. However, it fundamentally does not bear the mission of instructing life or representing the appeals of a certain class, so it cannot be said to have any consciousness.

During the period of translation, the translator received repeated assistance and guidance from Mrs. Tang Baochao (i.e., Princess Rong Ling), Mr. Yu Xunling, Mr. Tang Yunfan, and my brother Zeng Wei, and was also corrected from time to time by the readers, for which I am very grateful. What was especially fortunate was that the original author, Princess Der Ling, came to Shanghai and also corrected a few points herself, making the translation not only fully consistent with the original, but even more complete than the original.

Three months ago, Mr. Ma Yinliang, Mr. Zhou Shoujuan, and Mr. Huang Jiping of this newspaper informed me that because many readers were requesting reprints, and to give the effort I had put in over the past year and a half more purpose, they wanted me to reorganize, revise, and supplement the entire book so that a single-volume edition could be published in the shortest possible time. This was naturally something I was very happy to do, so I devoted more than twenty days to thoroughly reviewing and correcting it. Now it is finally finished. The illustrations in the book will also be enlarged or colorized. It is expected to be published next month.

Local Supplement of Shen Bao

Commentary

Premature Aging 205

— Zinan

Premature aging is one of the terminal illnesses of the Chinese people.

"Mature for his age" is the best compliment. The speaker strokes his beard and smiles, and the listener also has a pleased expression. And the person being praised, at this time, sits even more upright, becoming "mature" beyond measure.

A child who has just learned to walk is dressed in long robes and short jackets. When the child wants to play, he is pulled back and severely reprimanded.

Upon reaching the age of twenty, they begin to prepare for "longevity"; even longevity clothes, coffins, and burial grounds are being prepared.

"They hope for nothing but a stable life. Something in them, such as 'death is the meaningful moment of life,' and 'in the second half of human life, the normal psychology is the psychology of preparing for death.' Because of such assertions, death is regarded as a primitive idea, and they live a secluded life." (Gorky: On Drama.)

In China, the so-called "second half of human life" seems to come particularly early. Therefore, the so-called "preparation for death" is also "prepared" early, and "because of such assertions, death is regarded as a primitive idea, and they live a secluded life." Therefore, the desire to live a "secluded life" also comes particularly early, and because of the desire to live a "secluded life" early, "mature for his age" becomes the best "award" for young people.

Chinese people start preparing for death from the moment they are born. The so-called "prepare a coffin at the age of three, it will be useful when old" is exactly that.

However, this is truly the crystallization of the dying social psychology of aging petty citizens.

In response to this dying social psychology, we can look at Mr. Akita Ujaku's words: "Look, I am only in my fifties, compared to people in their sixties, I am still just a child."

Let's also look at Gide, Gorky, and Romain Rolland, who are "in their sixties," and how they are working hard for the future of humanity.

These are such good contrasts and such good lessons compared to the prematurely aging people who encourage "mature for his age"!

"We simply do not think about the time of death; we seize life from our own hands and guard it more quietly. It is extremely difficult work to fully open one's will and reason and value the constant heroic tension."

In a stagnant, prematurely aging society, this is truly the best remedy. We only have the right to survive in this society if we "seize life from our own hands and guard it more quietly."

However, "in our midst, there are still the unburied dead. They also eat, drink, walk on the streets, and breathe."

Moreover, before this prematurely aging society perishes, they will still "eat, drink, walk on the streets, and breathe," emitting a decaying miasma.

Page 16

Winter 206

— Hua Mu

Speaking of winter, some people will worry about it, while others will be very happy. The four seasons of the year do not inherently possess fixed advantages or disadvantages. The decision of love or hate depends entirely on one's environment, age, and breadth of mind. Each season follows the course of nature, alternating in cycles. To love spring and hate winter means enduring patiently, waiting for spring to arrive early and winter to pass quickly.

Now, the high-altitude hunting weather of the ninth month of autumn has finally completed its course in the seasons. According to the lunar calendar, it is the middle of October. Even if the weather hasn't become severely cold, and the north wind hasn't blown down snowflakes, according to the progression of the seasons, this boundless earth has already changed into a winter coat. In the near future, nature will gradually reveal winter's stern and cold face.

If the warm October weather in Jiangnan were seen by northerners, they might resent that nature is so partial, favoring one over the other. In the north, there is an ancient poem describing winter: "In the tenth month in barbarian lands, snow already flies." Though the seasonal segment is still early winter, October, it has lost the name and reality of early winter. Not long ago, Shanghai newspapers reported the blooming of winter peach blossoms. If this news were to reach the north, it would surely astonish and puzzle people, perhaps even leading to superstition, claiming it as an auspicious sign of a good year. Similar stories can be found in historical records. October is called Little Yangchun (Indian Summer), likely originating from this.

In my southern hometown, it doesn't snow in winter, and the trees remain evergreen throughout the year. The so-called Little Yangchun of October is much more deserving of the name. Many vegetable trees, such as peach, apricot, loquat, and pomegranate, will bloom at this time, but they rarely bear fruit. The only one that often bears fruit is the pomegranate, but not much, and the fruit is smaller and more astringent than those that ripen in summer. However, being able to obtain this summer fruit in early winter, October, naturally makes it seem more precious than usual.

If there is no snowy scenery to view in winter, it is naturally very dry, but the loveliness of winter lies precisely in this. A snowy day makes the north wind lose its majesty. The forest, standing all day in the howling northern wind, will dream more beautifully and sweetly of the spring buried in its branches. In the boundless, snow-white scenery, the beautiful face of winter is fully revealed. We do not see its desolation and ferocity, only boundless grandeur and radiance. Such a winter is out of the question in my southern hometown. However, the children there also feel that the arrival of winter is worth praising and welcoming, because what follows winter is still a more wonderful spring, and the universally celebrated, joyous New Year. Although they are not as fortunate as the children in Jiangnan and the North, who can have snowball fights in winter (the southern people are also warlike from a young age), they have dreams of New Year's joy constantly looming in their little minds, so they don't find the winter days too difficult to endure.

The Chinese New Year and the Western Christmas are both for children and are both set in winter, which greatly adds to the liveliness and vibrancy of winter. With snowy scenery, New Year, and Christmas in a cold and formidable winter, could one still be lonely?

The weather has suddenly turned cold in the past few days, and the sky filled with dense clouds looks like it's about to snow. Outside the window, the tung tree leaves appear even drier, more yellow, and weakly waiting to fall. The north wind sweeps across the overhead power lines, making a whooshing sound. Like hearing the footsteps of an old friend, a nameless comfort and joy suddenly rises in my heart. Winter, I have had an acquaintance with it. Now, I am indeed watching it stand gently before the window with a warm and affectionate smile.

Yes, winter has gently come to my door with an affectionate smile. At night, sitting alone in deep thought, I hear it knocking on my door with a very familiar tune and rhythm. It's a pity that there isn't a door knocker on the door, and there's a lack of an iron horse under the eaves. Otherwise, it would surely rock and beat out a very beautiful melody for me.

Winter has come. I believe my dreams will be more realistic, more beautiful, and more radiant.

Crow 207

— Er He

Perhaps this is my own peculiarity. I don't love orioles, I don't love yellow birds, but I love owls, but I love crows. The crow is a kind of bird that cannot please people, but the reason why I like it is because it cannot please people.

However, when I was young, I really hated crows. I hated that I could not exterminate them all. Behind my house, there were many elm trees and Chinese tallow trees. Among them, the one growing in the northwest corner was the largest and most majestic. There was a crow's nest on it. From the time I had memories, this crow's nest was always standing on that Chinese tallow tree, no matter spring, summer, autumn, or winter. In winter, the leaves had all fallen, so the crow's nest on the towering Chinese tallow tree could be seen from two or three miles away. If someone came to my house, and if they did not know the way, then they would ask a passerby. The passerby would say, "Oh, the Wen family? It's right there, in that big orchard with the crow's nest on the tall Chinese tallow tree." At the same time, they would point remotely with their hand. The visitor only needed to look for it according to what the passerby said.

Crows are considered unlucky things, so when we children heard a crow call, we would respond with the three words "Da Jia Hao" (which sounds similar to the crow's call) in a calm manner, or we would say, "Sharpen the scissors, kill the old crow!" "Boil the water, soak the old crow!" (Old crows are commonly referred to in my hometown.) to intimidate it. If it did not fly away, we would use long bamboo poles to intimidate it. In fact, we children did not understand anything. We only heard the elders say that a crow's call was an ominous sign, so we competed to be afraid. As soon as we heard a crow call, it seemed as if some danger would fall. We used words like "Sharpen the scissors" to intimidate the crow, but our mother often used the crow to intimidate us. For example, if we were playing happily, our mother would come over and say, "Jumping and jumping, having fun! A crow just called. I know you're all going to get beaten!" Then we would disperse, shouting, "Crow call, bad luck comes." Crow call, bad luck comes. (Bad luck, unfortunate news.) Sometimes, if we accidentally broke something, then we would really get beaten, but while enduring the pain with tears, we thought, "It's all the crow's fault. I must kill it!" Then we would clench our fists, showing a very determined look.

When I was young, I hated crows the same way. As I grew older and drifted in the city for many years, I gradually forgot that there was such a thing as a crow. This summer, I returned to my hometown and saw that the Chinese tallow tree was gone. Then I thought of that crow's nest. I asked my siblings who were about the same age, and they all said, "I don't know. That tree was cut down many years ago." They had probably forgotten their childhood long ago. I was just indifferent and didn't want to ask anything more.

After arriving here, I didn't think about crows either. But after all, it's late autumn and early winter now. In front of the school is the Confucius Forest, and my dormitory is behind the Confucius Temple. There are also several very large ginkgo trees behind the temple. So when I went out for a walk in the evening, I saw countless crows, their backs stained with the sunset, squawking in the Confucius Forest. At dawn, I again saw crows on the old ginkgo trees, their backs stained with the morning sun, squawking. However, I did not hate them, and of course, I did not have the childishness to say words like "Sharpen the scissors." I just felt a faint sadness attacking me. Sometimes, as I listened, listened, I almost suspected that the crow's call was my own voice.

These days it has been raining lightly, and the crows are especially loud. I am often disturbed by their squawking and have to put down the test papers I am grading and wander under the old ginkgo tree, humming in a low voice Nalan Xingde's poem: "The crows are gone, standing alone, who is to blame? The sudden snow turns the incense pavilion into catkins, the gentle breeze blows the prunus in the vase, and my heart is already ashes!" In silence, I feel that I am truly a crow. The crow, black all over, is a symbol of extreme sadness. Its being hated is not without reason. But at this moment, do I have a reason to hate it?

Listening to the crow's voice in the cold north wind - caw - caw - caw - how is it compared to reading a sad poem? From this, I understand that the oriole's and the yellow bird's being loved is not without reason either. There is really no need to stand up for the crow's being disliked, because it should be disliked.

Song Introduction 208

The Smiling Girl

In the dead of night, walking on the street, people come and go, flowing like water. In the dark alleys, a chorus of females, warbling like birds, giggling and chuckling, big and small, gaudy and green, beautiful and charming, pure and graceful, each adorned like a flower, with red sleeves. How hateful: the frivolous butterflies and mad bees, heartlessly ravaging, shamelessly insulting. The pain of ten months of pregnancy is in the mother's heart, so heartless and cruel, I advise you to reduce your cruelty. The people in the pit of fire, quickly save yourselves! Save yourselves! Save yourselves! Walk towards the bright path.

Dance halls and theaters, guesthouses and wine shops, crowded and bustling, carefree and unaware of sorrow. Graceful girls, considerate and gentle, exchanging glances, being intimate, tall and short, fat and thin, singing and dancing, swaying and twisting, each filled with boundless joy, hoarding it in their hearts. How pitiful: the bright flowers, heartlessly plucked, shamelessly caressed. The youthful years have long since flowed eastward, conscienceless and insane, I advise you to reduce your cruelty. The people in hell, quickly save yourselves! Save yourselves! Save yourselves! Walk towards the bright path.

Cheng Fangzhou Li Liansun Mao Jiashu

Opening: "The Difficulties of a Young Widow"

The red sun rises and illuminates the window, the beautiful woman gets up late and is too lazy to dress up, her whole body is clean and tidy, her haggard face has two lines of tears, without powder and rouge her eyebrows are tightly furrowed, she is a, young widow of Wen Jun, pondering and thinking, she adds autumn boredom, hateful husband is self-inflicted, was lured into the brothel, spent millions of gold and silver and sadly drove away the light, the family property is empty on all four walls, and the debt piles up day by day, worries are endless, creditors are pressing, the reputation is ruined and people hate, Qingbo's suicide makes the slave sad, poor me, crying until my heart is broken, lying alone on the bed at night, the bright brocade quilt is half empty, lonely and miserable, the morning chicken crows three times and I can't close my eyes, how can I dream of Huang Liang, three years of marriage is really short, and I can't bear to leave my slave to die, poor me, hard work with ten fingers can't get enough to eat, there is no overnight food in the house, the neighbor aunt came to me last night, since there is no daughter and no man, I advise you to remarry Zhang Baiwan in Dongcun, live in plenty and be happy, the current world is not the same as before, the chastity archway is not conspicuous, the difficulties have come to this point and my heart is confused, don't blame the beauty for not having any plans, listeners, what wonderful method can save the beautiful lady?

Xia Hesheng's Three Smiles

Opening: "The Mantis Making Friends"

The association aims to popularize harmonica music, so each score is finely printed on colored picture paper, and the cover is painted with various allegorical paintings for stage performance. Currently, as a preferential treatment for readers of this newspaper, anyone who clips the news and goes to the association's office at No. 10, Lane 157, Anren Street, East of the New North Gate in the city to request it will only be charged a partial cost of three cents per copy.

"Peach Blossoms After the Robbery" Begins Filming 215

In the bright spring, the most exciting thing is the peach blossoms. The bright and red color really makes people feel the preciousness of youth and the loveliness of nature. However, when the ruthless east wind blows, these poor peach blossoms wither. They drift aimlessly, allowing people to trample and play with them.

The scriptwriter of "Peach Blossoms After the Robbery" is the playwright Mr. Hong Shen, who studied in the United States. It was published in the "Literature" magazine in the past. Now, the Star Film Company is producing it into a film, directed by Zhang Shichuan, starring Hu Die and Gao Zhanfei. In "Peach Blossoms After the Robbery," the dream of the rise and fall of the homeland and the vicissitudes of personnel are all contained. As soon as the filming is completed, it can be presented to the audience. Wait for it!

About "Special Agent" 216

——Screened at the Grand Cathay——

Because of government orders, major Hollywood film companies produced a lot of bandit suppression films in 1935. The ones that have already been screened in Shanghai include Warner's "G-Men", Paramount's "The Lives of a Bengal Lancer", MGM's "The Great God Gold", and United Artists' "The Prisoner of Shark Island". From the perspective of both public opinion and box office, "G-Men" is of course the best. Now, Warner, the company that produced "G-Men," is once again showing its courage and filming "Special Agent," still directed by William Keighley, starring Bette Davis and George Brent. In "G-Men," hard machine guns are used to deal with the gangsters, but in "Special Agent," in addition to the hard machine guns, there are also soft women helping to probe for information and expose all the dark secrets in the bandit den. Therefore, the audience not only has fierce gunfights to watch, but also the wit of the female detective and the gangsters. This film is being screened at the Grand Cathay starting today. The left is the battlefield scene of the film.

Shen Bao Local Supplement Automobile Weekly

General Motors Has a Tendency to Merge with Nissan in Japan 219

— Shadowy Stalker

Japan's automobile industry. In recent years. Undoubtedly. Has made considerable progress. Their products. Numerically. Are increasing year by year. Not only in the domestic automobile market. Has it established a considerable position. Even in overseas markets. Starting with Eastern countries first. They are also vigorously promoting sales. Therefore. In the near future. Japan's automobile industry. Will have tremendous development. We can foresee this. However, from another perspective. Japan's automobile industry. Compared with Britain and the United States. Still seems very immature. In terms of products. It is certainly not as good as Britain and the United States. And the Japanese automobile factories. Currently only manufacture small cars. Only because the price is particularly low. Can they still be sold to Eastern countries. Otherwise, it would be difficult to compete in the world market.

The two giants of the American automobile industry. General Motors and Ford. Have branches everywhere overseas. In Japan. These two major car manufacturers. Also had branches established long ago. Their only purpose in establishing branches in various overseas countries. Is of course to reduce production costs. In overseas automobile markets. It is easier to promote sales. And among the same industry. Competition is also easier to win. Therefore. The establishment of this kind of branch. Although it has great benefits for oneself. For the host country. To put it bluntly. It is nothing more than a kind of economic aggression.

In Japan. A few years ago, there was basically no so-called automobile industry. Exactly the same as China at present. Completely no self-made cars. Therefore. Not much attention was paid to the establishment of factories by General Motors and Ford. But in recent years. Japan's automobile industry. Is rising. As mentioned above. Japanese automobile factories. In recent years, they have been limited to manufacturing small cars. But aren't Chevrolet from General Motors and V8 from Ford. Both low-priced small cars? Therefore. General Motors and Ford. Since there are branches in Japan. The result will certainly cause considerable impact and threat to the Japanese automobile industry. It will not be easy to rise.

Japan certainly will not ignore this issue. Therefore. The government. To protect the domestic automobile industry. Formulated a car industry bill. The most important two restrictions on foreign companies setting up factories in Japan are: (1) From now on. No new factories. Absolutely prohibited. Even factories that have already been established. After August 9 this year. No expansion of any equipment is allowed. (2) But if the company's capital. More than half is transferred to Japanese nationals. And the company's control is also transferred to the Japanese at the same time. The government may allow it to expand or add car plants. After reading the above clauses. We can clearly see the Japanese government's intention. To restrict the activities of foreign automobile factories establishing branches in Japan. It is tantamount to putting shackles on the heads of General Motors and Ford's Japanese branches. It is said that it will be implemented immediately after the next parliament passes it.

Since the Japanese government formulated this car industry bill. Ford. Expressed opposition. However, General Motors has expressed its willingness to merge with Nissan Motor Company. Nissan is considered to be one of the largest car factories in Japan. For the sake of various conveniences. General Motors also had talks with Nissan about cooperation last year. Therefore. The formulation of this car industry bill. Makes the merger of General Motors and Nissan even more possible. Currently, General Motors. Has drafted two solutions. (1) Transfer all company assets to Nissan. (2) Transfer 51% of the stock to Nissan. Important personnel from both sides. Have had many talks. But no decision has been made yet. And Nissan. Has to be instructed by the government. Only then can everything be decided. Presumably the merger of General Motors and Nissan. May become a reality. But it is only a matter of time.

New Information from the American Automotive Industry 220

— Ling Yun

Jenkins Plans to Break Campbell's Record. Since the Englishman Sir Malcolm Campbell achieved a car speed of 300 miles per hour, car racers around the world have admired him greatly. Now, there is a famous car racer named Jenkins in the southern United States. He is already planning a new racing car, preparing to break Campbell's record. His desired speed is 400 miles per hour, an increase of 100 miles compared to Campbell. The racing location is scheduled on the salt flats of Bonneville, Utah, around next autumn. Jenkins is currently in the hospital due to an injury and broken bones he sustained recently while racing in Nashville. He is a renowned racer, having won over 300 racing championships. The new racing car he is planning will have 24 cylinders, intending to surpass any land speed record. According to him, the car's horsepower is 3,600, while Campbell's engine only has 2,400 horsepower. It is propelled by four-wheel drive. He also said that the car is more streamlined than Campbell's "Bluebird." Each wheel is equipped with fin-like plates, ensuring that the wheels remain glued to the ground even at maximum speed. These plates can be adjusted, so whether a wheel needs more power or during turns, the plate can help it adhere tightly to the ground. Jenkins believes that the car can reach a speed of 400 miles per hour, or at least 350 miles per hour, gradually progressing to 400 miles per hour. He also believes that this will bring the world's highest car speed record back to the United States. The car's wheelbase is 170 inches. He estimates the engine's weight to be between 8,000 and 10,000 pounds. As for the Bonneville racing track, it is said to be the most perfect in the world, so he firmly believes that his wishes will not be in vain.

American Car Production in Nine Months. From January to September of this year, member factories of the American Automobile Manufacturers Association manufactured a total of 2,029,406 vehicles. This is a 15% increase compared to the same period last year. This number includes various passenger cars and trucks. However, it should be clarified that Ford's production is not included in the above total. Apart from that, almost all major manufacturers are included. The car production volume in September was relatively the lowest this year. According to the American Automobile Manufacturers Association, this is because car factories are preparing for the 1936 model cars. The new cars are planned to be unveiled at the National Automobile Show on November 2nd. According to the association's initial report, the car production volume in September was 57,860 vehicles, a 68% decrease compared to the 179,918 vehicles in August. Compared to September 1934, the decrease was 50%, as the car production volume in September last year was 116,649 vehicles.

New Cadillac and LaSalle Cars. The 1936 model Cadillac and LaSalle cars have been on display across the United States since last month. The current prices of these two cars are lower than before. The new Cadillac cars include the Sixty Series, Cadillac Fleetwood and Deville, and LaSalle. Their prices have been greatly reduced. Among them, the Sixty Series has entered the low-price car category, being the lowest price since the 1908 model four-cylinder car. The factory delivery price is $1,645 USD. According to factory officials, this car is specially designed for a group of people who need the excellence of a Cadillac body and a style that is convenient for personal use. The unique feature of this car is that it is easy to park, making it most suitable for women drivers. The Cadillac Fleetwood and Deville include V8, V12, and V16 engines. The beauty of the car body, the comfort of the ride, and the smoothness of the drive are all features of the new cars. The 1936 model LaSalle has a beautifully refined body that is most pleasing to the eye. Its driving performance and speed are said to be exceptionally perfect. Its price, factory delivery, is $1,175 to $1,255 USD. The Cadillac Sixty Series new car, equipped with a V8 engine, has 125 horsepower and very powerful engine.

What to Do When a Tire Goes Flat 221

— Lu Xue

Nowadays. Flat tires occurring unexpectedly. Happen very rarely. Normally speaking, if a hole is small. The air inside a balloon tire. Will of course not leak out quickly. Sometimes the driver notices the tire damage. Only after the car has driven for quite a distance after the tire has been damaged.

Even if the tire has such a hole. The car is still easy to drive. Because the air leaks out very slowly. In other words, the warning period is very long. If the driver is paying attention to the car body. He will feel vibrations while driving. These vibrations are due to the air leaking from the tire. At that time, he can change the wheel before the pressure is completely released.

There is one thing that must be especially stated here. That is, before changing the wheel. The car must be driven off the main road. We often see people changing wheels on narrow and busy roads. This not only obstructs traffic. And because of other vehicles coming and going. He is in danger of being knocked down. It is best to drive the car to a small road or corner away from the main road. When looking for this kind of small road or corner, you have to drive slower. Even driving for a mile or so. It will not harm the tires. Now new cars have permanently installed jacks. This is a great help when changing wheels. Not only can the wheel be changed quickly. And safe.

Sudden tire blowouts also happen. However, this tire must have been very weak to begin with. Or the tire casing has been carelessly used. For example. When a car drives over a sharp curb. The structure of the cords inside the tire casing will be damaged. If the tire is still used after being injured like this. The injured area is easily enlarged. Sometimes it even bulges outward. It is also very clear to see from the outside. If the car owner does not check his tires at that time. The air will bulge out from the weak spot. And the tire will deflate immediately.

In addition to the above-mentioned blowouts. Sometimes when a car accidentally drives over an inconspicuous obstacle. The air in the tire will suddenly leak out from a crack. But this happens very rarely. Therefore. Generally speaking. As long as we pay good attention to the tires. Blowouts will not happen.

However, drivers should know what to do in case a tire is damaged. Due to the sudden deflation. The rolling resistance of the tire will greatly increase. So the car is very easy to deviate from its normal course. If the damaged one is the front tire. Deviation is even more likely to occur. On wet roads. And it will also slip.

If the driver can hold the steering wheel steady. Even if there is unstable steering. It can usually be corrected immediately. As long as you use the appropriate force. Even if the steering mechanism vibrates. It is not difficult to make the car drive in the correct direction. Drivers sometimes drive very fast and only put one finger and thumb on the edge of the steering wheel. At that time, if the tire suddenly breaks down. It is impossible to avoid the danger of unstable steering.

In any emergency on the road. Ordinary people always apply the brakes vigorously first. But when a tire suddenly breaks down. This method must not be used. The function of the brakes is to hinder the movement of the wheels. So when the tire blows out, use the brakes. The result will separate the tire casing from the tire ring. This not only causes avoidable damage to the tire. And the metal tire ring rubs on the road. Strengthening the incorrect steering force. Even wrecking the wheel.

Sometimes when the tire is damaged and the situation requires the car to be driven slowly. For example, on a hillside. Then applying the brakes should be as gentle as possible. At the same time, the driver must hold the steering wheel tightly.

General Overview of Guangxi Highways 222

— Yong

Future Plans for Constructing Provincial Roads

Although Guangxi has over 12,000 li of completed highways. The routes in various regions are not fully connected. Water and land transportation. Are not fully connected to the main lines out of the province. The main lines out of the province are not fully connected. Future plans for constructing provincial roads. Externally, the main lines out of the province should continue to be completed. Internally, the routes in various regions should be connected and connected to major rivers. All provincial roads that should continue to be constructed have been predetermined and planned. They will be constructed in five years. In order to gradually complete them.

Roads to be Completed in the First Year

(1) Expedite the Qin Section of the Yongqin Road. This road starts from Tingzixu on the opposite bank of the Yonghe River to Wucun. It branches off from the Yonglong Road. From here, it travels south through Datang and Naxiao to the border of the province, Cekuangkui Xu. It connects to Guangdong Province via Xiaodong. To reach Qinzhou. It is the shortest and most important route for highways in southwestern provinces to reach the sea. This road is 220 li long within Guangxi. Although it is now fully open to traffic. The remaining 50 li from Dongkuang to Xiaodong within Qinxian has not yet been constructed. Over the years, we have repeatedly sent letters and telegrams urging. And repeatedly sent personnel to negotiate. And willing to allocate funds to assist. In order to complete it as soon as possible. But it has not yet been settled. This autumn, we will send personnel again to discuss solutions. Strive to complete it as soon as possible. So that the highways of the southwestern provinces. Reach the seaport early. To enrich the economy and strengthen national defense.

(2) Complete the Liuyong Road. This road is 180 li long. It is a branch of the Liugui Highway. It is also the middle section of the Liugui Road after the realignment. After the road is completed, the Liugui transportation will be 140 li shorter than the current Liuligui route. Both time and car costs are reduced and saved. Before the 16th year of the Republic of China, it was repeatedly surveyed. Only because of the obstruction of streams and rivers. The mountains are steep. The cost is huge and construction has been delayed for a long time. Recently, due to various needs. It needs to be completed urgently. Therefore, Changtang Village on the Liujiang River and the bridgehead of Dabai Lake were selected as the starting point. It passes through Huangmian, Sanlipo Village, and Ailing to Yongfu. It connects with the Guiyong Road. In February of this year, personnel were sent to measure. Construction is now starting from Changsanduan first. The entire line can be completed and open to traffic this year.

(3) Construct the Baidu Road. This road starts from Baise, passes through Luoli, Tianxi, Jiuzhou, and reaches the bank of the Badu River. It is 450 li long. The Badu River crosses into Ceheng in Guizhou. Passing through Anlong and Xingyi, it can reach Guiyang in the north. It connects to Kunming in the west. After this road is connected. The three provinces' political, military, cultural, and other aspects. Rely heavily on mutual assistance. And passengers and goods from Yunnan and Guizhou. Can also enter and exit through this line. The importance of the relationship. Should be on the Danchi Road that has been opened to traffic. And the Bailuo Road that will be built. The Bailuo and Danchi roads are limited to local transportation. Unable to connect the three provinces. To the line from Baidu into Guizhou and then into Yunnan. Within Guangxi, the land is relatively wide and flat along the way. And mostly clay. Therefore, although the route is more than twice as long as the Bailuo line. The required funds are only about 600,000 yuan more than the Bailuo line. The remaining section from Badu to Kunming. The project belongs to Yunnan and Guizhou provinces. Currently, the routes in both Yunnan and Guizhou have been under construction. At present, it has a rough scale and can be completed and opened to traffic this year. As for the line from Baise through Luoli, Tianxi, Jiuzhou, to Anlong and Xingyi in Guizhou Province and into Luoping in Yunnan Province. This was originally the Dianyu Railway. The original planned route of the Dianbai section. Now build a highway first. Then the construction of the railway in the future. The project will be easier to carry out. Therefore, after July of this year. Speed up the progress immediately. In order to complete and open to traffic in the autumn of next year.
